### [1] [Probing Hilbert space fragmentation using controlled dephasing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.13856)
*Dominik Vuina,Robin Schäfer,David M. Long,Anushya Chandran*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: Error


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Error

Method: Error

Result: Error

Conclusion: Error

Abstract: Dynamical constraints in many-body quantum systems can lead to Hilbert space fragmentation, wherein the system's evolution is restricted to small subspaces of Hilbert space called Krylov sectors. However, unitary dynamics within individual sectors may also be slow or non-ergodic, which limits experiments' ability to measure the properties of the entire sector. We show that additional controlled dephasing reliably mixes the system within a single Krylov sector, and that simple observables can differentiate these sectors. For example, in the strongly interacting XXZ chain with dephasing, the spin imbalance between even and odd sublattices distinguishes sectors. For appropriate choices of initial states, the imbalance begins positive, decays to a negative minimum value at intermediate times, and eventually returns to zero. The minimum reflects the average imbalance of the Krylov sector associated to the initial state. We compute the size of the minimum analytically in the limit of strong interactions, and validate our results with simulations at experimentally relevant interaction strengths.

</details>


### [2] [Connecting phases of matter to the flatness of the loss landscape in analog variational quantum algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.13865)
*Kasidit Srimahajariyapong,Supanut Thanasilp,Thiparat Chotibut*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过模拟不同量子相和初始化策略，展示了利用强而冷的初始化方法可以提高变量潜在的数量和训练过程中的可训练性，为模拟硬件上的量子变分算法提供了实用指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子变分算法（VQAs）在模拟量子硬件上的应用，寻找提高算法效率的方法。

Method: 通过分析不同热化和本地化相的量子绝热Ising链构建的VQA ansatz，研究其初始化策略和训练特性。具体包括调节混乱强度，研究不同相状态下的ansatz表达能力和损失方差的缩放特性。利用数值模拟，确定两个相中的最大表达能力发生在较大的M值，但温热相和MBL相在M较小时出现差异，温热相出现的退化步骤更早。通过利用这个间隙，提出分步初始化策略，即在中间M值开始初始化，在MBL区域进行初始化，以保持训练的可训练性同时保留足够的表达能力。

Result: 模拟显示，在温热相和MBL相中，最大的表达能力发生在较大的M值。温热相在较小的M中出现退化，而MBL相则在更大的M中能够找到合适的参数点。通过在中间M值进行初始化，可以在训练初期获得较优的训练轨迹。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了量子相变与量子变分算法的可训练性和表达能力之间的联系，并为实现模拟硬件上的量子变分算法提供了实用的初始化策略指导。

Abstract: Variational quantum algorithms (VQAs) promise near-term quantum advantage, yet parametrized quantum states commonly built from the digital gate-based approach often suffer from scalability issues such as barren plateaus, where the loss landscape becomes flat. We study an analog VQA ansätze composed of $M$ quenches of a disordered Ising chain, whose dynamics is native to several quantum simulation platforms. By tuning the disorder strength we place each quench in either a thermalized phase or a many-body-localized (MBL) phase and analyse (i) the ansätze's expressivity and (ii) the scaling of loss variance. Numerics shows that both phases reach maximal expressivity at large $M$, but barren plateaus emerge at far smaller $M$ in the thermalized phase than in the MBL phase. Exploiting this gap, we propose an MBL initialisation strategy: initialise the ansätze in the MBL regime at intermediate quench $M$, enabling an initial trainability while retaining sufficient expressivity for subsequent optimization. The results link quantum phases of matter and VQA trainability, and provide practical guidelines for scaling analog-hardware VQAs.

</details>


### [3] [Gravitational wave imprints on spontaneous emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.13872)
*Jerzy Paczos,Navdeep Arya,Sofia Qvarfort,Daniel Braun,Magdalena Zych*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: Few studies have addressed quantum gravity effects. A new experimental method shows how curved spacetime might change spontaneous emission in cold atoms. This could be detected in Fisher information experiments.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Interesting topic—combining quantum mechanics, relativity, and cold atoms for gravitational wave detection.

Method: Investigated a combined atom-field system in curved spacetime, looked at spontaneous emission modified by gravitational waves. Used Fisher information analysis.

Result: Shows the effect exists but is too small for current tech. Could be detected with future improvements.

Conclusion: May pave way for future tests of quantum gravity using cold atoms. Proof of principle, need more precise experiments.

Abstract: Despite growing interest, there is a scarcity of known predictions in the regime where both quantum and relativistic effects become observable. Here, we investigate a combined atom-field system in a curved spacetime, focusing specifically on gravitational-wave backgrounds. We show that a plane gravitational wave modifies spontaneous emission from a single atom, both in terms of sidebands in the spectrum and directionality of the emission. While the total decay rate remains unchanged, implying that no information about the gravitational wave is stored in the atomic internal state alone, the wave leaves imprints on the evolution of the composite atom-field system. To quantify how well this effect can be measured, we analyze both the classical Fisher information associated with photon number measurements and the quantum Fisher information. Our analysis indicates that the effect could be measured in state-of-the-art cold-atom experiments and points to spontaneous emission as a potential probe of low-frequency gravitational waves.

</details>


### [4] [Dynamical quantum phase transition with divergent multipartite entanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.13898)
*Jie Chen,Ricardo Costa de Almeida,Hendrik Weimer*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 研究了一个一维纵场伊辛模型在可积和不可积两个阶段中的非平衡退响应动力学，发现了新的动态量子相变，其 multipartite entanglement在临界时间出现发散，通过量子 Fisher信息量化，属于不同于基态相变的新的普遍类。通过频谱分析表明，这是由于系统多体动力学中激发态的constructive干涉导致的动态相变。并讨论了在冷库斯平台中的实验实现及在量子 metrology应用中有潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子相变和动态量子相变对理解量子系统的行为和开发新应用具有重要意义。

Method: 使用了一维纵场伊辛模型，研究了可积和不可积阶段中的退响应动力学，计算了系统中的 multipartite entanglement和量子 Fisher信息，进行了频谱分析，分析了动态相变的来源。

Result: 发现了动态量子相变，其性质不同于基态相变，并通过实验平台如冷库斯实现。

Conclusion: 这些发现扩展了量子相变理论，并为量子 metrology和量子信息处理提供了新方向。

Abstract: We investigate the nonequilibrium quench dynamics of the one-dimensional transverse-field Ising model in both integrable and nonintegrable regimes. In particular, we report on a novel type of dynamical quantum phase transition (DQPT) that is characterized by a divergent multipartite entanglement at critical times in the post-quench dynamics. We quantify the multipartite entanglement of the state by the quantum Fisher information and demonstrate that the DQPT belongs to a different universality class than the ground-state phase transition. Furthermore, we perform a spectral analysis of the DQPT and demonstrate that it is a genuine nonequilibrium transition arising from the constructive interference of excited states of the system during the many-body dynamics. Finally, we discuss potential experimental realizations in Rydberg platforms as well as applications in the context of quantum metrology.

</details>


### [5] [Fabrication of airbridges with gradient exposure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14565)
*Yuting Sun,Jiayu Ding,Xiaoyu Xia,Xiaohan Wang,Jianwen Xu,Shuqing Song,Dong Lan,Jie Zhao,Yang Yu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于梯度曝光的超导airbridge制造方法，该方法利用一层光致焦电阻层和梯度曝光技术精确控制airbridge的形状。与传统方法相比，该方法可以生产出无损耗、尺寸灵活的airbridge，从而更适合大规模超导量子电路的制造，并且简化了工艺步骤，提高了良品率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究关注于超导量子电路中airbridge的作用，airbridge是减少电感和互操作性干扰的关键组件。因此，如何高效可靠地制造airbridge成为研究 focus。

Method: 该论文采用了一种基于梯度曝光的制造方法，使用一层光致焦电阻层并通过梯度曝光来精确调控airbridge的结构。同时，通过调整曝光剂量和激光功率实现了对airbridge形状的精确控制，从而减少加工复杂度并提高良品率。

Result: 研究结果表明，采用该方法制造的airbridge具有无损耗、尺寸可调节的特点，特别适合大规模量子电路的制造。此外，该方法简化了工艺流程，显著提升了生产效率和质量。

Conclusion: 该论文的创新性在于提出了一种高效、灵活的airbridge制造技术，不仅简化了工艺流程，还显著提升了生产效率和产品质量。该方法为大规模超导量子电路的发展提供了重要支持。

Abstract: In superconducting quantum circuits, airbridges are critical for eliminating parasitic slotline modes of coplanar waveguide circuits and reducing crosstalks between direct current magnetic flux biases. Here, we present a technique for fabricating superconducting airbridges. With this technique, a single layer of photoresist is employed, and the gradient exposure process is used to define the profile of airbridges. In order to properly obtain the bridge profile, we design exposure dosage based on residual photoresist thickness and laser power calibrations. Compared with other airbridge fabrication techniques, the gradient exposure fabrication technique provides the ability to produce lossless superconducting airbridges with flexible size and, thus, is more suitable for large-scale superconducting quantum circuits. Furthermore, this method reduces the complexity of the fabrication process and provides a high fabrication yield.

</details>


### [6] [Detecting zero-point fluctuations with stochastic Brownian oscillators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.13952)
*Adrian E. Rubio Lopez,Felipe Herrera*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种增量噪声放大策略，以利用低品质量子振荡器探测环境零点波动。通过修正频率噪声，可以在恒温下放大量子偏差，用于检测环境参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高精度传感需要高质量量子振荡器，但低品质振荡器同样可能为环境参数监测提供新方法。

Method: 通过注入可控制的乘法频率噪声到布朗振荡器，放大量子偏差，用于检测环境参数。

Result: 在恒温下放大偏差，用振子能量或热流检测环境参数。

Conclusion: 低品质振荡器在有限温度下具有Exploring环境零点波动监测的能力。

Abstract: High-quality quantum oscillators are preferred over for precision sensing of external physical parameter because if the noise level due to interactions with the environment is too high, metrological information can be lost due to quantum decoherence. On the other hand, stronger interactions with a thermal environment could be seen a resource for new types of metrological schemes. We present a general amplification strategy that enables the detection zero-point fluctuations using low-quality quantum oscillators at finite temperature. We show that by injecting a controllable level of multiplicative frequency noise in a Brownian oscillator, quantum deviations from the virial theorem can be amplified by a parameter proportional to the strength of the frequency noise at constant temperature. As an application, we suggest a scheme in which the virial ratio is used as a witness of the quantum fluctuations of an unknown thermal bath, either by measuring the oscillator energy or the heat current flowing into an ancilla bath. Our work expands the metrological capacity of low-quality oscillators and can enable new measurements of the quantum properties of thermal environments by sensing their zero-point contributions to system variables.

</details>


### [7] [Universal cooling of quantum systems via randomized measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.11964)
*Josias Langbehn,George Mouloudakis,Emma King,Raphaël Menu,Igor Gornyi,Giovanna Morigi,Yuval Gefen,Christiane P. Koch*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 研究者模拟了自然冷浴，使用测量quettes逐渐冷却量子系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究者希望开发不需要提前系统能量谱信息的 Coolong 方式。

Method: 使用测量quettes，每个测量qubit与系统短暂交互。

Result: 无需系统谱知识的 Coolong 方案可行，当交互强度足够小时，等情况有效冷却量子系统。

Conclusion: 这一通用方案可应用于量子信息和模拟。

Abstract: It is generally believed that the design of cooling protocols requires knowledge of the system's spectrum. In contrast, cooling processes in nature occur whenever the system is coupled to a cold bath. But how does nature know how to cool quantum systems? Here we address this question by mimicking a natural cold bath with a reservoir of "meter" qubits that are initialized in their ground state and interact with the system sequentially for a specified time before being discarded. This protocol is equivalent to quantum measurements without keeping the measurement readouts. We show that a quantum system can be cooled without prior knowledge of the system's details when the interactions between the system and the meters, as well as the level splittings of the meters, are chosen randomly. For sufficiently small interaction strengths and long interaction times, the rotating-wave approximation becomes valid, ensuring that resonant energy-exchange processes, which lead to cooling, dominate over heating. This demonstrates that robust and scalable cooling of complex quantum systems can be achieved through generic, structure-independent protocols. Our findings thus offer a versatile universal framework for engineering, controlling, and manipulating quantum matter far from equilibrium, in particular, for the purposes of quantum information processing and quantum simulations.

</details>


### [8] [Fully Quantum Computational Entropies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14068)
*Noam Avidan,Thomas A. Hahn,Joseph M. Renes,Rotem Arnon*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种量子计算信息理论，并定义了量子计算极小和极大熵，探讨了其性质和应用，填补了量子信息理论中的计算效率缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着量子计算的快速发展，研究其计算效率和资源消耗的度量是必要的。

Method: 该论文通过构建新的量子计算熵，结合计算复杂度和效率，探索其性质，如数据处理定理和链式法则。它们还通过对偶关系定义了极大熵，并将其应用于量子位隔膜问题。

Result: 提出了新的量子计算极小和极大熵，并探讨了它们的性质，如数据处理和链式法则，极大熵还被应用为纠缠提取有效性的度量。

Conclusion: 该研究为量子信息论中加入计算效率和技术提供了框架和工具。这是量子计算不可或缺的基础。

Abstract: Quantum information theory, particularly its entropic formulations, has made remarkable strides in characterizing quantum systems and tasks. However, a critical dimension remains underexplored: computational efficiency. While classical computational entropies integrate complexity and feasibility into information measures, analogous concepts have yet to be rigorously developed in the quantum setting. In this work, we lay the basis for a new quantum computational information theory. Such a theory will allow studying efficient -- thus relevant in practice -- manipulation of quantum information. We introduce two innovative entropies: quantum computational min- and max-entropies (along with their smooth variants). Our quantum computational min-entropy is both the fully quantum counterpart of the classical unpredictability entropy, as well as the computational parallel to the quantum min-entropy. We establish a series of essential properties for this new entropy, including data processing and a chain rule. The quantum computational max-entropy is defined via a duality relation and gains operational meaning through an alternative formulation that we derive. Notably, it captures the efficiency of entanglement distillation with the environment, restricted to local quantum circuits of bounded size. With the introduction of our computational entropies and their study, this work marks a critical step toward a quantum information theory that incorporates computational elements.

</details>


### [9] [Comparing a Few Qubit Systems for Superconducting Hardware Compatibility and Circuit Design Sensitivity in Qiskit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14075)
*Hillol Biswas*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了不同量子位系统模拟器中的基底电路，以及在IBM Sherbrooke 127量子位处理器上实现的权衡分析。研究发现，选择更保守的基底电路设定，能够在更小规模的量子位数上获得更好的执行效率，同时对加工时间更为鲁棒。这为量子计算的实际应用提供了有价值的指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文章探究了在NISQ时代的量子计算中，如何在有限的硬件资源下平衡多个因素，如基底电路的通用性、设计参数的敏感性以及噪声的抗性。这将有助于量子计算在实际中的应用，特别是在资源紧张的条件下如何高效运行量子算法。

Method: 本文通过构建三个基底电路，分别针对不同量子位系统进行模拟，并与IBM Sherbrooke的127量子位处理器进行实验。通过比较不同基底电路在不同规模下的表现，研究噪声参数的空间分布及其影响因素。

Result: 研究结果表明，保守设定基底电路的参数在小规模量子位数下表现出更强的时间效率，并对参数的变化更具鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 论文提出了一种在实际应用中选择基底电路的方法，能够在有限的量子位资源下，提高量子算法的执行效率和可靠性。这有助于推动量子计算技术的进一步发展。

Abstract: In the current quantum computing ecosystem, building complex and integrated circuits for addressing real-world problems often involves using basic historical components like Bell states to take advantage of superposition, entanglement, and coherence. The availability of the simulator and the IBM quantum computing endeavor through Qiskit further broadens the scope of application based on domain use. In the NISQ era, however, error mitigation is a criterion that is applied when comparing a QPU run result with the simulator. As the real-world scope of application for quantum computing is being broadened, using simulators as a baseline offers confidence; however, concerns about computation resources and availability arise in the high-speed computational regime. As complex problems entail using a larger number of superconducting physical qubits, what should be the basis of framing a quantum circuit for building quantum algorithms in a real-world scenario, given hardware compatibility that should ideally provide confidence baselining with the simulator outcome? This work implements three base circuits for different qubit systems in the simulator and corresponding 127-qubit IBM Sherbrooke superconducting quantum processing units (QPU) to explore the tradeoff between generalizability, sensitivity of circuit design to parameters, noise resilience, resource planning, and efficient qubit usage insights.

</details>


### [10] [A Quantum Platform for Multiomics Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14080)
*Michael Kubal,Sonika Johri*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: A paper proposing a hybrid quantum-classical machine learning platform to model complex biological systems, addressing limitations in current computational approaches and quantum integration.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To tackle the complexity of biological systems and advance therapeutic interventions, leveraging emerging quantum computing technology.

Method: Combines quantum computing with machine learning using an encode-search-build approach.

Result: Demonstrates the platform's utility in quantum-enhanced classification and prediction of biological systems' evolution.

Conclusion: Validates the approach's potential through initial use cases, suggesting future scalability with more quantum resources.

Abstract: The complexity of biological systems, governed by molecular interactions across hierarchical scales, presents a challenge for computational modeling. While advances in multiomic profiling have enabled precise measurements of biological components, classical computational approaches remain limited in capturing emergent dynamics critical for understanding disease mechanisms and therapeutic interventions. Quantum computing offers a new paradigm for addressing classically intractable problems, yet its integration into biological research remains nascent due to scalability barriers and accessibility gaps. Here, we introduce a hybrid quantum-classical machine learning platform designed to bridge this gap, with an encode-search-build approach which allows for efficiently extracting the most relevant information from biological data to \underline{encode} into a quantum state, provably efficient training algorithms to \underline{search} for optimal parameters, and a stacking strategy that allows one to systematically \underline{build} more complex models as more quantum resources become available. We propose to demonstrate the platform's utility through two initial use cases: quantum-enhanced classification of phenotypic states from molecular variables and prediction of temporal evolution in biological systems.

</details>


### [11] [Certifying spatial entanglement between non-degenerate photon pairs with a camera](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14300)
*Emma Brambila,Raphael Guitter,René Sondenheimer,Markus Gräfe,Hugo Defienne*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 研究利用不同波长的光子对进行空间纠缠，并通过频率适配法测量相关性，发现在频率分立情况下，理论分析需调整以避免误判，且参数如泵腰宽度和晶体长度影响相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光子之间的空间纠缠在量子信息和通信中有广泛应用，理解不同参数对其的影响有助于优化相关实验和提高技术性能。

Method: 使用相机基于巧合技术测量光子对的对比度，自适应调整与频率相关的测量，通过爱因斯坦-波多尔斯基-罗森准则验证纠缠的存在。

Result: 通过调整参数，如泵腰宽度和晶体长度，观察到不同频率配对的纠缠性独立性，表明频率分立情况下需调整理论分析以避免误判。

Conclusion: 不同波长的光子对在空间纠缠上的新见解，频率适配法在纠缠检测中的有效性，以及参数调整对实验结果的影响。外，实验证明了在频率分立情况下，理论分析调整是必不可少的，以提高纠缠判断的准确性从而为量子通信奠定基础。

Abstract: We investigate transverse spatial entanglement between photon pairs of different wavelengths using a camera-based coincidence technique. By adapting the correlation measurements to the photons frequencies, we certify the presence of entanglement between the pairs through violation of an Einstein-Podolsky-Rosen criterion. Additionally, we examine how parameters such as pump waist and crystal length influence these correlations. Our results highlight key differences from the frequency-degenerate case, showing that an adapted theoretical analysis is essential to avoid significant misestimations and to reliably certify entanglement.

</details>


### [12] [The effect of partial post-selection on quantum discrimination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14105)
*Qipeng Qian,Christos N. Gagatsos*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 这项研究探讨了使用部分测量来增强无法正交的纯态间区分性能的可行性，发现部分测量无法提高平均区分性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子信息科学中态区分的重要性以及部分测量作为一种工具在量子工程中的应用前景。

Method: 通过构建一个一般性的框架，研究在部分测量后是否能通过经典通信来提高区分性能，使用POVM进行建模并计算最小错误概率。

Result: 部分测量和经典通信的结合无法降低平均区分错误概率，且等于不使用测量的原始情况。

Conclusion: 部分测量在该问题中没有提升区分性能的作用。

Abstract: The discrimination of quantum states is a central problem in quantum information science and technology. Meanwhile, partial post-selection has emerged as a valuable tool for quantum state engineering. In this work, we bring these two areas together and ask whether partial measurements can, on average, enhance the discrimination performance between two unknown and non-orthogonal pure states. Our framework is general: the two unknown states interact with the same environment-set in a pure state-via an arbitrary unitary transformation. A partial measurement is then performed on one of the output modes, modeled by an arbitrary positive operator-valued measure (POVM). We then allow classical communication to inform the unmeasured mode of the outcome of the partial measurement on the other mode, which is subsequently measured by a POVM that is optimal in the sense that the probability of error is minimized. The two POVMs act locally, but since we allow for classical communication between the two modes, we consider a scheme involving local operations and classical communication (LOCC). Under these considerations, we show that the minimum error probability, averaged over all possible conditional states, cannot be reduced below the minimum error probability of discriminating the original input states. In other words, prior state engineering via partial measurement does not improve the average discrimination performance.

</details>

This reveals a remarkable phenomenon: through nonperturbative interactions, entangled Unruh-DeWitt detectors can exhibit a dual effect-amplifying quantum coherence while degrading quantum entanglement. This finding stands in stark contrast to previous studies based on perturbative methods or Gaussian switching functions, which generally concluded that interactions between detectors and the field lead to a simultaneous degradation of quantum coherence and entanglement due to environmental decoherence. Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在量子计算中开发了高保真度的逻辑 ='magic state'，这对构建大规模的故障可容忍量子计算机至关重要。他们通过在 implode 计算机上fault-tolerant地制备一种逻辑 ='magic state'，并将其编码到 error-correcting 码中，展示了excellent 的保真度。研究的结果表明，该 quantum processor 已经达到了pseudo-threshold，从而提供了通用的故障可容忍计算基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现高保真度的逻辑 ='magic state' 是构建广泛使用故障可容忍计算的基础。在现有研究中，该工作首次展示了如何在 2D color code 之间进行 code switching，即将一种编码切换到另一种编码，以制备高保真度的逻辑 ='magic state'。这种实验方法展示了在 implode 计算机上的实际可行性，特别是在使用 Reed-Muller 码和 Steane 码进行切换的情况下。

Method: 研究者使用 fault-tolerant 的方法在 iod-trap quantum processor 上制备编码在 error-correcting 码中的逻辑 ='magic state'。他们展示了从 15-qubit 码到 7-qubit 码的 code switching 过程。研究包括准备好 Steane 码中的编码 ='magic state'，并计算出其保真度和 infidelity。他们利用两次复制的逻辑 Bell 测量来验证编码 ='magic state'。

Result: 研究结果表明在量子 implode 计算机上，编码 ='magic state' 的保真度很高，达到 82.58%。此外，研究者的保真度低于物理操作的主要误差率，表明量子 processor 已经超过伪阈值。这使得 2D color code 和 fault-tolerant 的 Clifford 码门组合成为功能完善的通用计算基元。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过故障可容忍地制备高保真度的逻辑 ='magic state' 并将其编码到 error-correcting 码中，以及在 implode quantum processor 上成功实现 2D color code 之间的 code switching，为实现大规模的故障可容忍量子计算提供了坚实的实证基础。这种结合不仅满足了目前计算需求，还为未来无法容忍的计算奠定了基础。

Abstract: Preparation of high-fidelity logical magic states has remained as a necessary but daunting step towards building a large-scale fault-tolerant quantum computer. One approach is to fault-tolerantly prepare a magic state in one code and then switch to another, a method known as code switching. We experimentally demonstrate this protocol on an ion-trap quantum processor, yielding a logical magic state encoded in an error-correcting code with state-of-the-art logical fidelity. Our experiment is based on the first demonstration of code-switching between color codes, from the fifteen-qubit quantum Reed-Muller code to the seven-qubit Steane code. We prepare an encoded magic state in the Steane code with $82.58\%$ probability, with an infidelity of at most $5.1(2.7) \times 10^{-4}$. The reported infidelity is lower than the leading infidelity of the physical operations utilized in the protocol by a factor of at least $2.7$, indicating the quantum processor is below the pseudo-threshold. Furthermore, we create two copies of the magic state in the same quantum processor and perform a logical Bell basis measurement for a sample-efficient certification of the encoded magic state. The high-fidelity magic state can be combined with the already-demonstrated fault-tolerant Clifford gates, state preparation, and measurement of the 2D color code, completing a universal set of fault-tolerant computational primitives with logical error rates equal or better than the physical two-qubit error rate.

Abstract: We investigate the impact of coherent control errors on quantum state evolution by deriving a general norm inequality based on Gronwall's lemma. This inequality provides an explicit upper bound on the deviation between an ideal quantum state and one subject to arbitrary coherent perturbations, including both time-dependent and time-independent cases. The framework is broadly applicable, requiring no assumptions about the detailed structure of the perturbation and full dynamics of the quantum system. We apply this approach to analyze the robustness of Grover's search algorithm in the presence of coherent errors. Our results characterizes quantitative scaling relations between the error strength, algorithm runtime, and success probability, offering practical guidelines for the design of resilient quantum protocols. We further compare the effects of time-dependent and time-independent perturbations, showing the distinctive ways in which coherent errors accumulate in quantum dynamics.

Abstract: Dynamical constraints in many-body quantum systems can lead to Hilbert space fragmentation, wherein the system's evolution is restricted to small subspaces of Hilbert space called Krylov sectors. However, unitary dynamics within individual sectors may also be slow or non-ergodic, which limits experiments' ability to measure the properties of the entire sector. We show that additional controlled dephasing reliably mixes the system within a single Krylov sector, and that simple observables can differentiate these sectors. For example, in the strongly interacting XXZ chain with dephasing, the spin imbalance between even and odd sublattices distinguishes sectors. For appropriate choices of initial states, the imbalance begins positive, decays to a negative minimum value at intermediate times, and eventually returns to zero. The minimum reflects the average imbalance of the Krylov sector associated to the initial state. We compute the size of the minimum analytically in the limit of strong interactions, and validate our results with simulations at experimentally relevant interaction strengths.

### [21] [Connecting phases of matter to the flatness of the loss landscape in analog variational quantum algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.13865)
*Kasidit Srimahajariyapong,Supanut Thanasilp,Thiparat Chotibut*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: This paper explores the use of variational quantum algorithms (VQAs) with analog quantum hardware, focusing on an array of quenched Ising chains. By tuning disorder strength, they examine two phases: thermalized and many-body localized (MBL). They find that in the thermalized phase, VQAs face 'barbarian' scaling issues at small M, but achieve maximum expressivity at larger M. In contrast, the MBL phase shows better barren plateau behavior. The authors propose initializing the system in the MBL phase to improve trainability without sacrificing expressivity, providing guidelines for scaling quantum algorithms on hardware. This work bridges quantum phases of matter with VQA optimization, offering practical insights for hardware implementation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Parametrized quantum states for VQAs face scalability issues like barren plateaus. This paper addresses this by studying a specific ansatz composed of quenched Ising chains in both thermalized and MBL phases. The aim is to find an optimal initialization strategy to mitigate training difficulties while maintaining expressivity.

Method: The authors investigate two phases of the Ising chain: thermalized and MBL. They numerically analyze the expressivity and loss variance scaling for each phase as parameters vary. They propose an MBL-based initialization method, which involves starting in the MBL phase at an intermediate M value to achieve better trainability and expressivity.

Result: In the thermalized phase, VQAs face-barbarian scaling issues leading to significant loss landscapes becoming flat (barber plateaus) at small M. In the MBL phase, better trainability is observed with no significant loss plateaus, despite requiring larger M for maximal expressivity. The MBL initialization strategy helps in achieving both expressivity and trainability.

Conclusion: This work links quantum phases of matter with the performance of variational quantum algorithms, providing practical guidelines for optimizing VQAs on analog quantum hardware by leveraging MBL phases for better trainability while maintaining maximal expressivity through appropriate initialization.

Abstract: Variational quantum algorithms (VQAs) promise near-term quantum advantage, yet parametrized quantum states commonly built from the digital gate-based approach often suffer from scalability issues such as barren plateaus, where the loss landscape becomes flat. We study an analog VQA ansätze composed of $M$ quenches of a disordered Ising chain, whose dynamics is native to several quantum simulation platforms. By tuning the disorder strength we place each quench in either a thermalized phase or a many-body-localized (MBL) phase and analyse (i) the ansätze's expressivity and (ii) the scaling of loss variance. Numerics shows that both phases reach maximal expressivity at large $M$, but barren plateaus emerge at far smaller $M$ in the thermalized phase than in the MBL phase. Exploiting this gap, we propose an MBL initialisation strategy: initialise the ansätze in the MBL regime at intermediate quench $M$, enabling an initial trainability while retaining sufficient expressivity for subsequent optimization. The results link quantum phases of matter and VQA trainability, and provide practical guidelines for scaling analog-hardware VQAs.

Result: 引力波改变原子自发辐射方向和谱峰，总衰减率不变，测量手段表明在现有技术下可行，可作为探测低频引力波的工具。

Abstract: Despite growing interest, there is a scarcity of known predictions in the regime where both quantum and relativistic effects become observable. Here, we investigate a combined atom-field system in a curved spacetime, focusing specifically on gravitational-wave backgrounds. We show that a plane gravitational wave modifies spontaneous emission from a single atom, both in terms of sidebands in the spectrum and directionality of the emission. While the total decay rate remains unchanged, implying that no information about the gravitational wave is stored in the atomic internal state alone, the wave leaves imprints on the evolution of the composite atom-field system. To quantify how well this effect can be measured, we analyze both the classical Fisher information associated with photon number measurements and the quantum Fisher information. Our analysis indicates that the effect could be measured in state-of-the-art cold-atom experiments and points to spontaneous emission as a potential probe of low-frequency gravitational waves.

Furthermore, we perform a spectral analysis of the DQPT and demonstrate that it is a genuine nonequilibrium transition arising from the constructive interference of excited states of the system during the many-body dynamics. Finally, we discuss potential experimental realizations in Rydberg platforms as well as applications in the context of quantum metrology.

Result: They present a method where by introducing noise, specific quantum deviations are amplified, allowing detection of thermal fluctuations through virial theorem deviations.

Conclusion: This approach extends the metrological capabilities of low-quality oscillators, enabling new ways to study quantum thermal environments.

Abstract: High-quality quantum oscillators are preferred over for precision sensing of external physical parameter because if the noise level due to interactions with the environment is too high, metrological information can be lost due to quantum decoherence. On the other hand, stronger interactions with a thermal environment could be seen a resource for new types of metrological schemes. We present a general amplification strategy that enables the detection zero-point fluctuations using low-quality quantum oscillators at finite temperature. We show that by injecting a controllable level of multiplicative frequency noise in a Brownian oscillator, quantum deviations from the virial theorem can be amplified by a parameter proportional to the strength of the frequency noise at constant temperature. As an application, we suggest a scheme in which the virial ratio is used as a witness of the quantum fluctuations of an unknown thermal bath, either by measuring the oscillator energy or the heat current flowing into an ancilla bath. Our work expands the metrological capacity of low-quality oscillators and can enable new measurements of the quantum properties of thermal environments by sensing their zero-point contributions to system variables.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机可能是探索如何有效地冷却量子系统，尤其是当缺乏系统谱知识时，寻找一种无依赖的方法，自然过程如何通过辅助系统解热。

Method: 研究方法是通过辅助子系综模拟自然冷源，系统与辅助子系统逐个互动，时间为持续时间，没有保留测量结果，模拟无测量解热过程。利用随机 chose 的相互作用和能级间隔，应用旋转波近似确保解热为主过程。

Result: 研究结果表明，当相互作用强度较小且时间足够长时，旋转波近似有效，解热主导，实现了对复杂量子系统的高效低温控制。这对于量子计算和模拟有重要应用价值。

Abstract: It is generally believed that the design of cooling protocols requires knowledge of the system's spectrum. In contrast, cooling processes in nature occur whenever the system is coupled to a cold bath. But how does nature know how to cool quantum systems? Here we address this question by mimicking a natural cold bath with a reservoir of "meter" qubits that are initialized in their ground state and interact with the system sequentially for a specified time before being discarded. This protocol is equivalent to quantum measurements without keeping the measurement readouts. We show that a quantum system can be cooled without prior knowledge of the system's details when the interactions between the system and the meters, as well as the level splittings of the meters, are chosen randomly. For sufficiently small interaction strengths and long interaction times, the rotating-wave approximation becomes valid, ensuring that resonant energy-exchange processes, which lead to cooling, dominate over heating. This demonstrates that robust and scalable cooling of complex quantum systems can be achieved through generic, structure-independent protocols. Our findings thus offer a versatile universal framework for engineering, controlling, and manipulating quantum matter far from equilibrium, in particular, for the purposes of quantum information processing and quantum simulations.

### [31] [The effect of partial post-selection on quantum discrimination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14105)
*Qipeng Qian,Christos N. Gagatsos*

Main category: quant-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: LOCC 无法改善 Discrimination 平均性能，下界由输入态决定。

Conclusion: 局部测量和经典通信无法提高未知纯态的 Discrimination 能力。

Abstract: The discrimination of quantum states is a central problem in quantum information science and technology. Meanwhile, partial post-selection has emerged as a valuable tool for quantum state engineering. In this work, we bring these two areas together and ask whether partial measurements can, on average, enhance the discrimination performance between two unknown and non-orthogonal pure states. Our framework is general: the two unknown states interact with the same environment-set in a pure state-via an arbitrary unitary transformation. A partial measurement is then performed on one of the output modes, modeled by an arbitrary positive operator-valued measure (POVM). We then allow classical communication to inform the unmeasured mode of the outcome of the partial measurement on the other mode, which is subsequently measured by a POVM that is optimal in the sense that the probability of error is minimized. The two POVMs act locally, but since we allow for classical communication between the two modes, we consider a scheme involving local operations and classical communication (LOCC). Under these considerations, we show that the minimum error probability, averaged over all possible conditional states, cannot be reduced below the minimum error probability of discriminating the original input states. In other words, prior state engineering via partial measurement does not improve the average discrimination performance.

This reveals a remarkable phenomenon: through nonperturbative interactions, entangled Unruh-DeWitt detectors can exhibit a dual effect-amplifying quantum coherence while degrading quantum entanglement. This finding stands in stark contrast to previous studies based on perturbative methods or Gaussian switching functions, which generally concluded that interactions between detectors and the field lead to a simultaneous degradation of quantum coherence and entanglement due to environmental decoherence. Notably, while initially separable detectors successfully harvest quantum coherence from the vacuum, entanglement extraction remains fundamentally prohibited. These contrasting behaviors underscore the fundamental distinction between coherence and entanglement as quantum resources, and highlight their complementary roles in field-detector interactions.

Abstract: Multipass cells are critical components in a variety of quantum technologies, including atomic magnetometers and optical quantum memories, due to their ability to achieve long optical paths within compact volumes. In optical magnetometry, increasing the optical depth through multipass geometries enhances sensitivity by reducing photon shot noise and enabling quantum nondemolition (QND) detection. In this work, we present a novel recirculating multipass alkali cell that improves the active-to-cell volume ratio and minimizes beam spot overlap, thereby addressing spin noise limitations inherent in conventional cylindrical Herriott cavity designs. We develop and validate an analytical model based on the ABCD matrix method to predict beam spot positions, sizes, and astigmatism effects, with results confirmed through Zemax simulations. In addition, we introduce a general analytical model for analyzing spin correlation noise in multipass alkali cells, incorporating both astigmatism and spatial intensity distribution-features not addressed in existing models. Method: 论文采用量子陷阱处理器的实验方法，利用编码和切换技术，从十五位的量子reed-muller码切换到七位的steane码，生成了高失真率的逻辑魔法态。

Result: 实验结果表明，生成的逻辑魔法态失真率低于物理操作的最高失真率至少2.7倍，证明处理器的性能已接近阈值。同时，在同一处理器上创建了两个编码魔法态，并进行了逻辑贝尔基测量，验证了编码魔法态的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究为构建大规模容错量子计算机提供了关键的技术突破，突破了色码之间的切换限制，提升了量子计算的基础能力。

Abstract: Preparation of high-fidelity logical magic states has remained as a necessary but daunting step towards building a large-scale fault-tolerant quantum computer. One approach is to fault-tolerantly prepare a magic state in one code and then switch to another, a method known as code switching. We experimentally demonstrate this protocol on an ion-trap quantum processor, yielding a logical magic state encoded in an error-correcting code with state-of-the-art logical fidelity. Our experiment is based on the first demonstration of code-switching between color codes, from the fifteen-qubit quantum Reed-Muller code to the seven-qubit Steane code. We prepare an encoded magic state in the Steane code with $82.58\%$ probability, with an infidelity of at most $5.1(2.7) \times 10^{-4}$. The reported infidelity is lower than the leading infidelity of the physical operations utilized in the protocol by a factor of at least $2.7$, indicating the quantum processor is below the pseudo-threshold. Furthermore, we create two copies of the magic state in the same quantum processor and perform a logical Bell basis measurement for a sample-efficient certification of the encoded magic state. The high-fidelity magic state can be combined with the already-demonstrated fault-tolerant Clifford gates, state preparation, and measurement of the 2D color code, completing a universal set of fault-tolerant computational primitives with logical error rates equal or better than the physical two-qubit error rate.

### [36] [Norm Inequality for Perturbed Quantum Evolutions and Its Application to Grover's Algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14230)
*Kohei Kobayashi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了相干误差对量子态演化的影响，通过Gronwall引理导出一般范数不等式，得到理想量子态和受任意相干扰动的量子态之间偏差的显式上界估计。这种方法适用于各种相干扰动和量子系统动力学，无需详细结构假设。然后将此方法应用于分析Grover搜索算法在相干误差下的鲁棒性，得出误差强度、算法运行时间及其成功概率之间的关系，为设计有抗干扰能力的量子协议提供了指导。最后比较了时变和时不变扰动对量子动力学累积效应的不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子计算中的误差控制是非常重要的，尤其是对关键算法如Grover搜索的理解。通过分析相干误差对量子态的影响，可以制定更有效的 Quantum Error Correction 和容错设计策略。

Method: 论文利用Gronwall引理建立泛函不等式，用于估计理想态与受扰态之间的偏差。这种方法适用于各种类型和强度的相干误差，并不依赖于具体系统结构。然后将该不等式应用于Grover搜索算法，分析其在不同误差下的稳健性，得到误差、运行时间和成功概率之间的量化关系。

Result: 论文得出，随着错误强度增加或运行时间延长，Grover算法的成功概率会降低。对于时变和时不变的错误，累积效应不同，时间依赖的错误可能导致更大的偏差。这些结果为设计具备抗干扰能力的量子协议提供了明确的指导和优化依据。

Conclusion: 该研究通过泛函不等式分析了量子算法的鲁棒性，拓展了处理各种相干误差的通用方法。对于未来研究，可以考虑引入机器学习进行误差校正自动化设计，并优化现有抗干扰策略。此外，将这种分析方法扩展到其他关键量子算法和实验系统是值得探索的方向。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of coherent control errors on quantum state evolution by deriving a general norm inequality based on Gronwall's lemma. This inequality provides an explicit upper bound on the deviation between an ideal quantum state and one subject to arbitrary coherent perturbations, including both time-dependent and time-independent cases. The framework is broadly applicable, requiring no assumptions about the detailed structure of the perturbation and full dynamics of the quantum system. We apply this approach to analyze the robustness of Grover's search algorithm in the presence of coherent errors. Our results characterizes quantitative scaling relations between the error strength, algorithm runtime, and success probability, offering practical guidelines for the design of resilient quantum protocols. We further compare the effects of time-dependent and time-independent perturbations, showing the distinctive ways in which coherent errors accumulate in quantum dynamics.

Abstract: A range of quantum algorithms, especially those leveraging variational parameterization and circuit-based optimization, are being studied as alternatives for solving classically intractable combinatorial optimization problems (COPs). However, their applicability is limited by hardware constraints, including shallow circuit depth, limited qubit counts, and noise. To mitigate these issues, we propose a hybrid classical--quantum framework based on graph shrinking to reduce the number of variables and constraints in QUBO formulations of COPs, while preserving problem structure.
  Our approach introduces three key ideas: (i) constraint-aware shrinking that prevents merges that will likely violate problem-specific feasibility constraints, (ii) a verification-and-repair pipeline to correct infeasible solutions post-optimization, and (iii) adaptive strategies for recalculating correlations and controlling the graph shrinking process. We apply our approach to three standard benchmark problems: Multidimensional Knapsack (MDKP), Maximum Independent Set (MIS), and the Quadratic Assignment Problem (QAP).

These findings demonstrate a scalable pathway for applying near-term quantum algorithms to classically challenging constrained optimization problems.

Abstract: Quantum computing has attracted a lot of attention in recent years. It is one of the promising candidates for the next-generation computing paradigms. Basically, there are two technical lines to realize quantum computing. One is composing the unitary operators of a few qubits to achieve general unitary operators on an arbitrary number of qubits, known as the approach of quantum circuits. Although the results in the note are not peer reviewed, we would like to make them public because they are quite easy to check.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The challenge of atom loss in neutral atom quantum processors has been a significant obstacle for scaling up quantum computing. Managing this loss is crucial as it contributes to a major fraction of errors. The paper addresses this gap by proposing an efficient method to replace lost atoms quickly, which allows for deeper and more reliable quantum circuits.

Method: The approach involves creating a continuously loaded reservoir near the computation zone. Atom extraction is done using tweezers at a rate of up to 500 times per second. This process allows for the preparation of new qubit arrays simultaneously, integrating operations like single-atom preparation and non-destructive imaging. The metastable Yb qubits ensure that existing qubits are not disturbed during this process due to their isolation from thermal and imaging light sources.

Result: The implementation enables the creation of qubit arrays 30 times per second, significantly increasing the efficiency of quantum processing. This method removes the bottleneck of atom loss, allowing for deep quantum circuits. The technique achieves high rates and ensures that the quantum states remain undisturbed, contributing to more reliable quantum computations.

Conclusion: The paper presents a foundational method for implementing fast and deep quantum circuits using neutral atoms. By solving the atom loss problem with a continuous replacement reservoir, the approach paves the way for scalable, fault-tolerant quantum computing. The isolation of metastable Yb qubits ensures the integrity of quantum operations, marking a crucial step towards practical quantum technologies.

Abstract: Neutral atom quantum processors are a promising platform for scalable quantum
computing. An obstacle to implementing deep quantum circuits is managing atom
loss, which constitutes a significant fraction of all errors. Current
approaches are either not capable of replacing lost atoms in the middle of a
circuit -- and therefore restricted to fixed, short circuit depths -- or
require more than an order of magnitude longer time than gate and measurement
operations to do so. In this work, we demonstrate fast, continuous atom
replacement leveraging the metastable $^{171}$Yb qubit. A continuously loaded
reservoir near the computation zone enables on-demand atom extraction with
tweezers up to 500 times per second. New qubit arrays can be prepared 30 times
per second when including single-atom preparation, non-destructive imaging and
initialization. Importantly, existing qubits are completely undisturbed by the
reloading process, owing to the extreme isolation of the metastable qubit from
cooling and imaging light. This work establishes a complete foundation for
implementing fast quantum circuits with unlimited depth, removing a final
roadblock for fault-tolerant quantum computing with neutral atoms.

Abstract: The plausible resolution of the Casimir puzzle implying that the dissipative

field of the magnetic dipole oscillating near a metallic surface is computed

evanescent waves. By comparing with the case of graphene, whose dielectric
response is spatially nonlocal and possesses the double pole at zero frequency,

Method: 采用理论分析，设计两种实验方案：量子钟干涉装置和纠缠产生机制。

Result: 实验方案不可行，效果微小。

Conclusion: 鉴于目前技术限制，无法可靠探测这些效应，需要更高级技术或更大规模实验。但研究为量子引力测试提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Understanding physical phenomena at the intersection of quantum mechanics and
general relativity remains a major challenge in modern physics. While various
experimental approaches have been proposed to probe quantum systems in curved
spacetime, most focus on the Newtonian regime, leaving post-Newtonian effects
such as frame dragging largely unexplored. In this study, we propose and
theoretically analyze an experimental scheme to investigate how post-Newtonian
gravity affects quantum systems. We consider two setups: (i) a quantum clock
interferometry configuration designed to detect the gravitational field of a
rotating mass, and (ii) a scheme exploring whether such effects could mediate
entanglement between quantum systems. Due to the symmetry of the configuration,
the proposed setup is insensitive to Newtonian gravitational contributions but
remains sensitive to the frame-dragging effect. Assuming the validity of the
quantum equivalence principle, this approach may provide insights not only into
the quantum nature of gravity but also into whether spacetime itself exhibits
quantum properties. However, our analysis reveals that, within realistic
experimental parameters, the expected effects are too small to be detected. We
discuss possible interpretations of this undetectability, and its implications
for tests of quantum gravity.

### [47] [The logical structure of contextuality and nonclassicality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15071)
*Songyi Liu,Yongjun Wang,Baoshan Wang,Chang He,Jinchng Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores quantum contextuality and its relation to nonclassicality, proposing a mathematical framework based on logic algebra. They conclude that contextuality is sufficient but not necessary for nonclassicality and present experiments that noncontextual systems can demonstrate nonclassicality. They also highlight simplifications in detecting contextuality with fewer measurements.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the relationship between quantum contextuality and nonclassicality is important for advancing quantum theory and its applications, such as quantum computing and cryptography.

Method: The study uses logic algebra to create a framework for comparing classical and quantum experiments. The mathematical approach allows for precise characterization of contextuality and nonclassicality, and the authors demonstrate specific experimental setups to showcase their findings.

Result: The key findings include that contextuality is a sufficient but not necessary condition for nonclassicality. Additionally, they present examples of quantum experiments that exhibit nonclassical behavior without requiring contextuality, such as quantum systems with only 3 measurements demonstrating contextuality, fewer than previously required in some cases.

Conclusion: This work provides a deeper understanding of the foundational aspects of quantum mechanics, particularly contextuality and nonclassicality. The proposed framework and experimental results open new possibilities for both theoretical exploration and practical applications in quantum technology.

Abstract: Quantum contextuality is known as the fundamental feature of quantum
mechanics. It is not clear whether contextuality fully reveals the nonclassical
aspects of quantum mechanics. To answer this question, we propose a
mathematical framework based on logic algebra to compare classical and quantum
experiments. With the framework, we precisely characterize the contextuality
and nonclassicality, reveal that the former is a sufficient but not necessary
condition for the latter, and present a type of quantum experiments which
exhibit nonclassicality without contextuality. We also point out that the
property of quantum systems is captured by the projector generators. Therefore,
it is possible to witness quantum contextuality with simplified measurement
configurations. For example, we show that 12 projectors witness the
Kochen-Specker contextuality, and 3 measurements are sufficient to witness the
quantum contextuality, as compared to the 4 presented in the compatibility
graph approach.

</details>


### [48] [Improving Quantum Battery Capacity in Tripartite Quantum Systems by Local Projective Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15074)
*Yiding Wang,Hui Liu,Shao-Ming Fei,Tinggui Zhang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过局部von Neumann测量在三体量子系统中对量子电池容量的影响进行了研究，提出了两种测量基底协议，并引入了最优局域投影算子的概念。作者给出了这些协议在一般三体X态下的具体解析表达式，并分析了白噪声和去相噪声对该电池容量的负面影响，并证明通过最优局部投影算子可以增强子系统和整体系统的电池容量。通过数值例子验证了不同方案在容量提升方面的效果，结果显示局部von Neumann测量是一种有效的提升多体量子系统电池容量的工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该论文涉及量子电池的研究，量子电池在量子信息处理和量子计算中具有重要作用。研究如何提升量子电池的容量和 Robustness 对于量子技术的发展具有重要意义。

Method: 论文研究了局部von Neumann测量在三体量子系统中的影响，提出了两种测量基底协议，并通过引入最优局域投影算子的概念，得出了在一般三体X态下的解析表达式。并分析了不同噪声对电池容量的影响，证明了优化测量能够提高系统的 Robustness。数值例子的仿真验证了结论。

Result: 论文得出结论：局部von Neumann测量能够有效提升三体量子系统的电池容量，并且在不同噪声影响下表现出一定的 Robustness。优化的测量基底在提升电池容量和增强系统的 Robustness 方面效果显著。

Conclusion: 该论文通过局部von Neumann测量研究了三体量子系统的电池容量问题，提出了有效的测量基底设计方案，并展示了在不同噪声环境下的 Robustness。研究结果表明，局部测量是一种有效的工具来提升量子电池的容量和 Robustness。这种研究方法为量子电池的设计和优化提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The impact of local von Neumann measurements on quantum battery capacity is
investigated in tripartite quantum systems. Two measurement-based protocols are
proposed and the concept of optimal local projective operators is introduced.
Specifically, explicit analytical expressions are derived for the protocols
when applied to general three-qubit X-states. Furthermore, the negative effects
of white noise and dephasing noise on quantum battery capacity are analyzed,
proving that optimal local projective operators can improve the robustness of
subsystem and total system capacity against both noise types for the general
tripartite X-state. The performance of different schemes in capacity
enhancement are numerically validated through detailed examples and it is found
that these optimized operators can effectively enhance both subsystem and total
system battery capacity. The results indicate that the local von Neumann
measurement is a powerful tool to enhance the battery capacity in multipartite
quantum systems.

### [49] [Excitation Amplitude Sampling for Low Variance Electronic Structure on Quantum Computers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15438)
*Connor Lenihan,Oliver J. Backhouse,Tom W. A. Montgomery,Phalgun Lolur,M. J. Bhaseen,George H. Booth*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 研究结合经典启发式和部分影射量子态 tomography，设计高效量子设备上的电子系统信息提取方案。证明了该方法能大幅减少所需的测量次数，同时对噪声非常 robust，适用于实际量子设备，特别是大的系统。此外，还在量子嵌入框架下扩展了这一方法，用于计算金属氧化物的自旋能隙体积依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation:  extracted information from quantum devices is crucial for various quantum algorithms and applications, particularly in materials science. However, due to the complex nature of correlated electronic systems, existing methods may not be efficient enough. This paper aims to address this challenge by combining classical heuristics with partial shadow tomography to improve efficiency and robustness.

Method: The method involves using a correlation energy functional and sampling a set of excitation amplitudes from the quantum state. Additionally, partial shadow tomography is employed to reduce the number of measurements needed while maintaining statistical accuracy. The approach also integrates quantum embedding frameworks to handle beyond-energy properties, improving stability and applicability to realistic systems.

Result: The results show that the proposed protocols significantly reduce the number of measurements required, achieving up to two orders of magnitude reduction in measurement shots. This reduction allows for handling larger system sizes. Moreover, the methods demonstrate high resilience to quantum device noise, with up to an order of magnitude increase in noise tolerance compared to traditional techniques. Efficient scaling is maintained even in the presence of noise, indicating robust performance. The ability to extract beyond-energetic properties, such as spin gaps in Nickel Oxide, further extends the applicability of these methods, showing potential in solving practical materials science problems.

Conclusion: The paper presents novel protocols for extracting information from quantum devices by combining classical heuristics with partial shadow tomography, which offer significant efficiency gains and enhanced noise resilience, particularly beneficial for dealing with large and realistic correlated systems in quantum computing and materials science. The success in handling beyond-energetic properties further validates the broader applicability of these methods in advancing quantum technologies for complex scientific challenges.

Abstract: We combine classical heuristics with partial shadow tomography to enable
efficient protocols for extracting information from correlated ab initio
electronic systems encoded on quantum devices. By proposing the use of a
correlation energy functional and sampling of a polynomial set of excitation
amplitudes of the quantum state, we can demonstrate an almost two order of
magnitude reduction in required number of shots for a given statistical error
in the energy estimate, as well as observing a linear scaling to accessible
system sizes. Furthermore, we find a high-degree of noise resilience of these
estimators on real quantum devices, with up to an order of magnitude increase
in the tolerated noise compared to traditional techniques. While these
approaches are expected to break down asymptotically, we find strong evidence
that these large system arguments do not prevent algorithmic advantage from
these simple protocols in many systems of interest. We further extend this to
consider the extraction of beyond-energetic properties by mapping to a coupled
cluster surrogate model, as well as a natural combination within a quantum
embedding framework. This embedding framework avoids the unstable
self-consistent requirements of previous approaches, enabling application of
quantum solvers to realistic correlated materials science, where we demonstrate
the volume-dependence of the spin gap of Nickel Oxide.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子相干性检测与测量的重要性，促进量子信息技术的发展。

Method: 基于部分转置的方法、非线性探测策略及其适用性分析，提供相干稳健性下界估计。

Result: 提出新准则、策略和下界分析，提升检测和量化相干性的方法。

Conclusion: 结果为量子理论增添新进展，促进相关技术发展。

Abstract: Quantum coherence is one of the most basic characteristics of quantum
mechanics. Here we give some methods to detect and measure quantum coherence.
Firstly, we propose a coherence criterion without full quantum state tomography
based on partial transposition. Moreover, we present a coherent nonlinear
detection strategy from witnesses, in which we find that for some coherent
states, normal witness detection fails but our nonlinear detection succeeds. In
addition, we prove that when the nonlinear detection on the two copies of the
coherent state fails, the nonlinear detection on the three copies may be
successful. Finally, due to the difficulty in calculating robustness of
coherence for general states, we introduce a lower bound for coherent
robustness based on the witness operator, and after comparing our lower bound
with the currently known lower bound, one show that our lower bound is better.
Coherence is believed to play a crucial role in quantum information tasks,
making the detection and quantization of coherence particularly significant.
Therefore, these results help to open up new avenues for advancement in quantum
theory.

### [51] [Aperiodic Dissipation as a Mechanism for Steady-State Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15108)
*Shilpi Roy,Jiangbin Gong*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 找到一种新的、无规律的耗散机制，让量子系统中的局部化效果容易控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了让耗散不再破坏量子系统，开始探索耗散如何 actually帮助量子效应，比如控制局域化。

Method: 通过模态比和相位参数的不均一分析，分别研究两种无规律耗散的情况，找到最有效的局域化方式。

Result: 发现在适度无规律的耗散下，量子系统局部化效果显著，且通过干扰预测和实证计算，验证了耗散如何主动塑造局域化。

Conclusion: 无规律耗散是一个有效的工具来调控开放量子系统中的局域化现象，为量子调控和设计新的量子相开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Dissipation is traditionally regarded as a disruptive factor in quantum
systems because it often leads to decoherence and delocalization. However,
recent insights into engineered dissipation reveal that it can be tuned to
facilitate various quantum effects, from state stabilization to phase
transitions. In this work, we identify aperiodic dissipation as a mechanism for
inducing steady-state localization, independent of disorder or a quasiperiodic
potential in the Hamiltonian. This localization arises from long-range phase
correlations introduced by a spatially varying dissipation phase parameter,
which enables nontrivial interference in the steady-state. By systematically
comparing two classes of aperiodic dissipation (defined as commensurate and
incommensurate cases), we find that incommensurate modulation plays the most
efficient role in stabilizing a localized steady-state. Our analysis, based on
coherence measures, purity, and participation ratio, reveals a direct link
between eigenstate coherence and real-space localization, showing that
dissipation can actively shape localization rather than simply causing
decoherence. These findings highlight aperiodic dissipation as a viable
approach to controlling localization in open quantum systems, potentially
enabling new ways to manipulate quantum states and design dissipation-driven
phases.

Method: Optimal compilation strategies tailored for QFT circuits and NAQC systems are introduced. These strategies minimize atom movements, achieving theoretical lower bounds while preserving high circuit fidelity.

Result: The proposed methods outperform state-of-the-art compilers, serving as benchmarks for evaluating NAQC compiler performance.

Conclusion: The proposed methods effectively address the challenge of implementing QFT in NAQC by optimizing atom movements and maintaining high circuit fidelity, providing benchmarks for future NAQC compiler development.

Abstract: Neutral-atom quantum computing (NAQC) offers distinct advantages such as
dynamic qubit reconfigurability, long coherence times, and high gate
fidelities, making it a promising platform for scalable quantum computing.
Despite these strengths, efficiently implementing quantum circuits like the
Quantum Fourier Transform (QFT) remains a significant challenge due to atom
movement overheads and connectivity constraints. This paper introduces optimal
compilation strategies tailored to QFT circuits and NAQC systems, addressing
these challenges for both linear and grid-like architectures. By minimizing
atom movements, the proposed methods achieve theoretical lower bounds in atom
movements while preserving high circuit fidelity. Comparative evaluations
against state-of-the-art compilers demonstrate the superior performance of the
proposed methods. These methods could serve as benchmarks for evaluating the
performance of NAQC compilers.

### [53] [A Topologically Fault-Tolerant Quantum Computer with Four Dimensional Geometric Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15130)
*David Aasen,Matthew B. Hastings,Vadym Kliuchnikov,Juan M. Bello-Rivas,Adam Paetznick,Rui Chao,Ben W. Reichardt,Matt Zanner,Marcus P. da Silva,Zhenghan Wang,Krysta M. Svore*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The authors are advancing topological quantum coding by leveraging geometric dimensions to enhance memory stability across quantum hardware scales, focusing on practical applications in both near-term and utility quantum computing environments.

Method: Four-dimensional self-correcting quantum memory geometry is employed, code constructions are developed with a specific generator, and leakage is minimized using topological methods. The design includes a universal error correction architecture with logical operations achievable in a single logical round, achieved through lattice codes with minimal stabilizers and manageable syndrome extraction depths.

Result: The proposed codes, such as the [[96,6,8]] lattice code, exhibit high pseudo-thresholds, low logical error rates, and efficient gate operations, demonstrating robustness under circuit-level noise. The architecture supports universal, fault-tolerant operations with low overhead, and the codes adapt to different quantum hardware with optimal parameters.

Conclusion: The paper deliverable is a universal quantum computing architecture enhanced by four-dimensional topological codes, offering scalability, efficient error correction, and reduced resource demands, positioning it as a key advancement in achieving fault-tolerant quantum computing.

Abstract: Topological quantum codes are intrinsically fault-tolerant to local noise,
and underlie the theory of topological phases of matter. We explore geometry to
enhance the performance of topological quantum codes by rotating the four
dimensional self-correcting quantum memory, and present codes targeted to both
near-term and utility-scale quantum computers. We identify a full set of
logical Clifford operations and with it design a universal fault-tolerant
quantum architecture. Our design achieves single-shot error correction,
significant reductions in required qubits, and low-depth logical operations. In
turn, our proposed architecture relaxes the requirements for achieving fault
tolerance and offers an efficient path for realization in several near-term
quantum hardware implementations. Our [[96,6,8]] 4D Hadamard lattice code has
low weight-6 stabilizers and depth-8 syndrome extraction circuits, a high
pseudo-threshold of $\sim 0.01$, and a logical error rate of $\sim 10^{-6}$ per
logical qubit per round of error correction at $10^{-3}$ physical error rate
under a standard circuit-level noise model. A Clifford-complete logical gate
set is presented, including a constructive and efficient method for Clifford
gate synthesis.

blahblahblahblahblahblahblahblahblahblahblahblah

Abstract: We show that the $T$-depth of any single-qubit $z$-rotation can be reduced to
$3$ if a certain catalyst state is available. To achieve an
$\epsilon$-approximation, it suffices to have a catalyst state of size
polynomial in $\log(1/\epsilon)$. This implies that
$\mathsf{QNC}^0_f/\mathsf{qpoly}$ admits a finite universal gate set consisting
of Clifford+$T$. In particular, there are catalytic constant $T$-depth circuits
that approximate multi-qubit Toffoli, adder, and quantum Fourier transform
arbitrarily well. We also show that the catalyst state can be prepared in time
polynomial in $\log (1/\epsilon)$.

*Jipeng Wang,Joscha Hanel,Zenghui Jiang,Raphael Joos,Michael Jetter,Eddy Patrick Rugeramigabo,Simone Luca Portalupi,Peter Michler,Xiao-Yu Cao,Hua-Lei Yin,Shan Lei,Jingzhong Yang,Michael Zopf,Fei Ding*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 项链分布（QKD）在实际光纤中面临很多麻烦，比如极性问题和色散。时间编码虽然有优势，但还没有在确定性单光子源中得到实验证明。这项研究填补了这一空白，展示了量子点光源的潜力。

Method: 他们用高亮度量子点光源，在 telecom-wavelength上发出单光子，通过时间编码实现了QKD。实验显示120km光纤中安全稳定，超过6小时。

Conclusion: 这项研究表明，基于量子点的可靠光源对于实现强大的量子密钥分发至关重要，为大规模量子通信奠定了基础。

Abstract: Quantum key distribution (QKD) with deterministic single photon sources has
been demonstrated over intercity fiber and free-space channels. The previous
implementations relied mainly on polarization encoding schemes, which are
susceptible to birefringence, polarization-mode dispersion and
polarization-dependent loss in practical fiber networks. In contrast, time-bin
encoding offers inherent robustness and has been widely adopted in mature QKD
systems using weak coherent laser pulses. However, its feasibility in
conjunction with a deterministic single-photon source has not yet been
experimentally demonstrated. In this work, we construct a time-bin encoded QKD
system employing a high-brightness quantum dot (QD) single-photon source
operating at telecom wavelength. Our proof-of-concept experiment successfully
demonstrates the possibility of secure key distribution over fiber link of 120
km, while maintaining extraordinary long-term stability over 6 hours of
continuous operation. This work provides the first experimental validation of
integrating a quantum dot single-photon source with time-bin encoding in a
telecom-band QKD system. In addition, it demonstrates the highest secure key
rate among the time-bin QKDs based on single-photon sources. This development
signifies a substantial advancement in the establishment of a robust and
scalable QKD network based on solid-state single-photon technology

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The discussion on whether gravity must be quantized is a deep fundamental question in physics, pushing for innovative theories that bridge classical and quantum physics while addressing their limitations.

Method: The researchers used a hybrid system of a qubit and a classical particle to simulate and analyze the inconsistencies in conservation laws within completely positive dynamics.

Result: The study revealed violations of angular momentum conservation despite rotational symmetry in the equations, indicating issues with conservation laws in hybrid theories.

Conclusion: While hybrid classical-quantum approaches show promise, their limitations, such as broken conservation laws, suggest the need for more consistent frameworks to properly integrate quantum mechanics into gravitational theories without compromising foundational physical principles.

Abstract: Whether gravity must be quantized remains one of the biggest open problems in
fundamental physics. Classical-quantum hybrid theories have recently attracted
attention as a possible framework in which gravity is treated classically yet
interacts consistently with quantum matter. Schemes based on completely
positive dynamics satisfy most formal consistency requirements and enable a
systematic treatment of quantum backreaction, but they also give rise to
features that challenge conventional physical intuition, such as the breakdown
of conservation laws. To illustrate this issue, we consider a qubit interacting
with a classical particle and demonstrate that the corresponding hybrid system
violates angular momentum conservation despite the rotational symmetry of the
underlying equations of motion.

Method: 研究者通过分析多维参数空间中的测量关系和参数相关性，推导出精确的估计不确定性原理，然后开发了一种几何方法（误差椭圆）来辅助理解。

Result: 获得了一个适用于两种参数估计的紧致不确定性关系，并将其应用于复色相空间中的位移估计，证明了多参数估计可以通过参数空间几何的调整来提高精度。

Abstract: Quantum multiparameter estimation aims to simultaneously estimate multiple
parameters from observing quantum systems and data processing. The complexity
of quantum multiparameter estimation arises primarily from measurement
incompatibility and parameter correlations. By manipulating the
multidimensional parameter space, we derive an estimation uncertainty relation
that captures the impact of measurement incompatibility and parameter
correlation on quantum two-parameter estimation. This uncertainty relation is
tight for pure states and completely describes the quantum limit of
two-parameter estimation precision. We also develop an error ellipse method to
intuitively illustrate the impact of the uncertainty relation and apply it to
the phase-space complex displacement estimation. Our research shows that
multiparameter estimation challenges can be effectively addressed by
manipulating the geometry of multidimensional parameter space.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: The researchers constructed a traversable wormhole analog using the SYK model and TFD state, implemented in a quantum circuit. They manipulated parameters like temperature (β) and the position of the message qubit, compared fidelities between the SYK-based and TFIM-based protocols, and analyzed the protocol for different β values and SWAP operator. Abstract: This study aims to provide insights into various aspects of quantum chaos and

traversable wormhole utilizing the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model in conjunction
with the Thermofield Double (TFD) state framework, implemented within a quantum
circuit. Subsequently, we manipulate various parameters, including temperature
($\beta$) and the location of the message qubit, and compare the fidelity
result with that of the Transverse Field Ising Model (TFIM)-based
wormhole-inspired teleportation protocol. Our findings demonstrate that the
SYK-based protocol achieves a higher fidelity of states in comparison to the
TFIM counterpart. We further analyze the protocol for different values of
$\beta$ and the SWAP operator. These findings are attributed to the emergence
of random matrix ensembles via random phase theory within the dynamics of the

state, followed by teleportation across the system. We introduce a Pauli
stabilizer-based fidelity measure to diagnose the teleportation
characteristics. This yields a considerable enhancement in fidelity relative to
the single-qubit variant of the protocol. Finally, we analyze the temporal
fluctuation of fidelity for both single-qubit and two-qubit message across the
channel, contributing to a deeper understanding of quantum teleportation
dynamics.

### [60] [Observation of Kardar-Parisi-Zhang universal scaling in two dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.15521)
*Simon Widmann,Siddhartha Dam,Johannes Düreth,Christian G. Mayer,Romain Daviet,Carl Philipp Zelle,David Laibacher,Monika Emmerling,Martin Kamp,Sebastian Diehl,Simon Betzold,Sebastian Klembt,Sven Höfling*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: The study observes 2D KPZ scaling in exciton-polariton condensates, confirming their role as an equilibrium-free platform for nonequilibrium universality.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to confirm the KPZ universality class in 2D through experiments, highlighting non-equilibrium states which are less understood.

Method: Momentum-resolved photoluminescence spectroscopy and space/time-resolved interferometry were used to analyze phase correlations in these quantum fluids.

Result: The results show scaling exponents matching 2D KPZ predictions, thus confirming the universality class.

Conclusion: Exciton-polariton condensates provide a reliable system for researching 2D nonequilibrium behavior, broadening our understanding of complex quantum systems out of equilibrium.

Abstract: Equilibrium and nonequilibrium states of matter can exhibit fundamentally
different behavior. A key example is the Kardar-Parisi-Zhang universality class
in two spatial dimensions (2D KPZ), where microscopic deviations from
equilibrium give rise to macroscopic scaling laws without equilibrium
counterparts. While extensively studied theoretically, direct experimental
evidence of 2D KPZ scaling has remained limited to interface growth so far.
Here, we report the observation of universal scaling consistent with the KPZ
universality class in 2D exciton-polariton condensates -- quantum fluids of
light that are inherently driven and dissipative, thus breaking equilibrium
conditions. Using momentum-resolved photoluminescence spectroscopy as well as
space- and time-resolved interferometry, we probe the phase correlations across
microscopically different systems, varying drive conditions in two distinct
lattice geometries. Our analysis reveals correlation dynamics and scaling
exponents in excellent agreement with 2D KPZ predictions. These results
establish exciton-polariton condensates as a robust experimental platform for
exploring 2D nonequilibrium universality quantitatively, and open new avenues
for investigating the emergence of coherence in interacting quantum systems far
from equilibrium.
